Authentic Chinese Restaurant with a Great Atmosphere. From the humble exterior, I didn't expect it to be a well furnished space inside. It seems like I'm entering a historical Chinese building. There are several areas that you can seat. There are private rooms for dinners with special guests.

I was surprised by the brochure that gives a historical glimpse of Chengdu. This is a great cultural touch.

The food is great. The price is a bit on the high side. I ordered tea and they provided a very high quality tea that's meant to be enjoyed slowly. Service was a bit slow on the day we went, but it isn't something to complain about,<//Text>

<review>If you're looking for a high end & authentic szechuan restaurant, this is one of the best places for that in the area. Maybe it's because I haven't had good Chinese food before but I was never a big fan of that cuisine... til my friend from China recommended this place and now my friends and I find every excuse to eat here HEHE.

The 2 MUST ORDERS are the crispy chicken and the mapo tofu. My friend from the OC is so obsessed with the crispy chicken that she tries to come here every weekend just for that. The light broth of the pork soup balanced the spiciness of the other entrees. I was pleasantly surprised at how good the panda rice ball dessert was. The black bean paste inside of it and the water/syrup that it's floating in have a very subtle sweetness to it.

They remodeled this place and the interior is really modern, minimalistic, and clean. The first floor is the waiting area and the dining area is upstairs. There are rooms you can reserve for a big party. This would be a nice place for a first date but tbh I would imagine conversation to be a struggle bc of how damn spicy the meals are lol.<//review><gmap_id>0x80c2dbc2b4bd57f9:0x36126cb67bcb6e8d</gmap_id><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNQ1zUfElb7w350s6IrIoeaDRGnGTnPg3I2cSBb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOCRvOgn0PqdXOXlmUEW_gGIks3A6Jdwjmaw5Xz=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPAYiK7rNLgYtYu7RtPQOIftYUyylf9hdtVqUc5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMKtHocivDjxG_u5E99DzNs7zfIQYlMIy8iRYVI=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< userid>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
This is a beautiful restaurant with great food and excellent service.  The food preparation and seasoning is authentic, which is due to the restaurants roots in Chengdu, but it is also carefully prepared and nicely presented.

We ordered the Chengdu Dan Dan Mian which was especially tasty because the seasoning was so well balanced.  We also ordered the Ma Po Tofu because it is one of the signature dishes.  It was rich tasting and nicely spicy with the Szechuan pepper providing the tongue tingling.

The service was superior to most any other Chinese restaurant in the area, with the manager checking in with us at the end of the meal to see how we liked the food.

This restaurant is excellent in every respect.</review>

<rate>1<//rate>< text>
DO NOT GO TO THIS CREDIT UNION.

This is a long time coming but I think it is time for my review of this place. This used to be my go-to credit union, however they messed up BADLY.

I moved to Sacramento and thought it would to nice to keep this as my credit union since they were serving me well. One day when I tried to use my debit card, it was rejected. I keep my information private so it caught me off guard on how my information was compromised for this rejection.

I looked into my bank statements and found out that some new debit card was issued under my account and more than 500 dollars was used! I had major panic and anxiety of these fraudulent charges. I immediately changed all my passwords and googled all the ways to lock up your information. I was all in my head on how my information was compromised.

I called customer support and they said that did not know what is going on, they suggested for me to talk to my family. After calling my family, I learned that this bank issued the new card to my FATHER. I called back and they locked the card. They did not know how my dad got a new card issued under my name since they ask for ID when reporting a lost card/issue a new one.

They mailed me a new card which took a few days to arrive. So I was out of a debit card for a few days along with the panic I had. They returned the money that my dad used and charged him instead.

Not only that this was extremely inconvenient to me and my father, all this bank said was "sorry".

I will be cancelling my membership to this credit union soon. I can't stand that they did nothing to address the inconvenience. If the branch looks into my description of my case, they will know exactly who I am.

I did talk to Shonna at the time of incident. All she said was that they will train their staff so that this kind of mistake will not happen again. Nothing  to address my inconvenience.< /text>

< text>
I brought my small dog in for an annual exam. Dr. Hynes examined her and brought her to the back for routine procedures (vaccines, blood draw, nail trim). My dog has never had a problem behaving for procedures in the past, and although nervous, has never been difficult while being worked on at other clinics.

While my dog was in the back with the technicians I heard her screaming for a prolonged period of time. It was so disturbing I finally poked my head out of the door and asked someone if she was ok. They replied, “ She’s fine; they are just working on her” as she continued to scream. They eventually brought her back and when I asked what happened the tech said, “She started creaming when she saw the nail clippers.”

I have clipped her nails several times myself and have never seen such a reaction. I thought maybe they clipped her nails too short and hurt her nail. But her nails looked fine. I didn’t believe their story, but I let it go and went home.

Later in the day I noticed her tail was swollen and bent in an awkward position. She was very uncomfortable and couldn’t raise her tail. I called the clinic and sent them photos and a video of her tail. They agreed to see her in the morning.

I spoke with Dr. Hymes about what I heard while they were working on my dog. She was not present at the time (which is normal). It’s the tech’s job to due routine procedures.

I shared my concern that something may have happened to her while being restrained. Dr. Hynes was immediately defensive and said I was being disrespectful for insinuating that they hurt my animal.

I asked Dr. Hymes to hold a meeting with her staff to make sure everyone is on the same page when it comes to handling animals. I would also expect that if something goes wrong, they would communicate that to the pet owner immediately. These ideas were brushed aside.

I was given a multitude of reasons why she could have screamed, but none of them included that it could have been due to an injury. As to how her tail was injured, I was given other wild ideas such as, “Maybe it’s a mast cell tumor”.

Dr. Hymes was more interested in defending herself and her staff than admitting the possibility that something could have gone wrong. Her focus should have been rebuilding the trust I lost in them and making a simple promise to have a talk with the staff.  We will not be going back.</text>

Dr. Diamond is an excellent veteranarian and has taken care of at least 6 of my various pets that I have had. He listens to your questions and answers them in a most professional manner. Dr. Tritt works hand in hand with him and is a very worthy vet herself.
There is nothing I can say but I am thankful to have such a great pet clinic close to me. The staff is wonderful and also very caring, taking each pet personally like it is their own. If you want a vet, this is the place.

< Review>
The restaurant is nice inside and seats are comfortable. The salad bar is not outstanding but very good. Try the spaghetti and meatballs; delicious! The macaroni and cheese is good but too soft and creamy. Good if you don't have teeth! The Rice Krispie treat looked good but was dry; need to add more marshmallow cream for sure. The ice tea is great; it's not weak, just right. Service is friendly; big smiles. Good place to dine alone or with a group. If you're in a wheelchair, it's somewhat difficult opening the door. Handicap accessible entrance would be a smart idea.< /Review>
